1% move\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        if not self.ib.nextOrderId:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        #                         "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\nimport datetime\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBKRWrapper(EWrapper):\n    def __init__(self, data_queue):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.data_queue = data_queue\n        self.order_id = None\n        self.account = None\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.order_id = orderId\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        # Pass bar data to the queue for the main thread\n        self.data_queue.put(('historicalData', reqId, bar))\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId, start, end):\n        self.data_queue.put(('historicalDataEnd', reqId, start, end))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        self.data_queue.put(('error', reqId, errorCode, errorString))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                    permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.data_queue.put(('orderStatus', orderId, status, filled, avgFillPrice))\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.data_queue.put(('execDetails', reqId, execution))\n\nclass IBKRClient(EClient):\n    def __init__(self, wrapper):\n        EClient.__init__(self, wrapper)\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.prices = []\n\n    def update(self, price):\n        self.prices.append(price)\n        if len(self.prices) > self.lookback:\n            self.prices.pop(0)\n\n    def signal(self):\n        if len(self.prices) < self.lookback:\n            return None  # Not enough data\n        # Simple momentum: buy if price > lookback average, sell if < lookback average\n        avg = sum(self.prices[:-1]) / (self.lookback - 1)\n        last = self.prices[-1]\n        if last > avg:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif last < avg:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return None\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    def __init__(self, gui, host, port, client_id):\n        self.gui = gui\n        self.data_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.wrapper = IBKRWrapper(self.data_queue)\n        self.client = IBKRClient(self.wrapper)\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.client_id = client_id\n        self.connected = False\n        self.strategy = None\n        self.running = False\n        self.reqId = 1\n        self.contract = None\n        self.position = 0  # 1 for long, -1 for short, 0 for flat\n        self.last_signal = None\n\n    def connect(self):\n        try:\n            self.client.connect(self.host, self.port, self.client_id)\n            threading.Thread(target=self.client.run, daemon=True).start()\n            # Wait for nextValidId\n            while self.wrapper.order_id is None:\n                time.sleep(0.1)\n            self.connected = True\n            self.gui.log(\"Connected to IBKR TWS.\")\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.gui.log(f\"Connection failed: {e}\")\n            return False\n\n    def disconnect(self):\n        self.client.disconnect()\n        self.connected = False\n        self.gui.log(\"Disconnected from IBKR TWS.\")\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol, secType, exchange, currency):\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = secType\n        contract.exchange = exchange\n        contract.currency = currency\n        return contract\n\n    def start(self, symbol, secType, exchange, currency, lookback, bar_size, quantity):\n        if not self.connected:\n            self.gui.log(\"Not connected to IBKR TWS.\")\n            return\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy(lookback)\n        self.contract = self.create_contract(symbol, secType, exchange, currency)\n        self.quantity = quantity\n        self.running = True\n        self.position = 0\n        self.last_signal = None\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.reqId += 1\n        self._run_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True)\n        self._run_thread.start()\n        self.gui.log(\"Bot started.\")\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.running = False\n        self.gui.log(\"Bot stopped.\")\n\n    def run(self):\n        while self.running:\n            # Request historical data for the last N bars\n            endDateTime = \"\"\n            durationStr = f\"{self.strategy.lookback} D\" if self.bar_size.endswith(\"day\") else f\"{self.strategy.lookback * 2} mins\"\n            self.client.reqHistoricalData(\n                self.reqId,\n                self.contract,\n                endDateTime,\n                durationStr,\n                self.bar_size,\n                \"TRADES\",\n                1, 1, False, []\n            )\n            bars = []\n            bars_received = 0\n            bars_needed = self.strategy.lookback\n            done = False\n            # Collect historical data\n            while not done and self.running:\n                try:\n                    item = self.data_queue.get(timeout=5)\n                    if item[0] == 'historicalData' and item[1] == self.reqId:\n                        bar = item[2]\n                        bars.append(bar.close)\n                        bars_received += 1\n                    elif item[0] == 'historicalDataEnd' and item[1] == self.reqId:\n                        done = True\n                    elif item[0] == 'error':\n                        self.gui.log(f\"Error: {item[3]}\")\n                        done = True\n                except queue.Empty:\n                    self.gui.log(\"Timeout waiting for historical data.\")\n                    done = True\n\n            if len(bars) >= self.strategy.lookback:\n                for price in bars[-self.strategy.lookback:]:\n                    self.strategy.update(price)\n                signal = self.strategy.signal()\n                if signal and signal != self.last_signal:\n                    self.execute_trade(signal)\n                    self.last_signal = signal\n                self.gui.log(f\"Latest close: {bars[-1]:.2f}, Signal: {signal}\")\n            else:\n                self.gui.log(\"Not enough historical data.\")\n            time.sleep(60)  # Wait for next bar\n\n    def execute_trade(self, signal):\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = signal\n        order.orderType = \"MKT\"\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        # Only trade if position is not already in direction\n        if signal == 'BUY' and self.position <= 0:\n            self.client.placeOrder(self.wrapper.order_id, self.contract, order)\n            self.position = 1\n            self.gui.log(f\"Placed BUY order for {self.quantity}.\")\n            self.wrapper.order_id += 1\n        elif signal == 'SELL' and self.position >= 0:\n            self.client.placeOrder(self.wrapper.order_id, self.contract, order)\n            self.position = -1\n            self.gui.log(f\"Placed SELL order for {self.quantity}.\")\n            self.wrapper.order_id += 1\n        else:\n            self.gui.log(f\"No trade executed. Already in position: {self.position}\")\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"IBKR Momentum Trading Bot\")\n        self.bot = None\n\n        # Connection Frame\n        conn_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(root, text=\"Connection\")\n        conn_frame.pack(fill='x', padx=10, pady=5)\n        ttk.Label(conn_frame, text=\"Host:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='w')\n        self.host_var = tk.StringVar(value=\"127.0.0.1\")\n        ttk.Entry(conn_frame, textvariable=self.host_var, width=12).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(conn_frame, text=\"Port:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='w')\n        self.port_var = tk.IntVar(value=7497)\n        ttk.Entry(conn_frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(conn_frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4, sticky='w')\n        self.client_id_var = tk.IntVar(value=1)\n        ttk.Entry(conn_frame, textvariable=self.client_id_var, width=4).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        self.connect_btn = ttk.Button(conn_frame, text=\"Connect\", command=self.connect)\n        self.connect_btn.grid(row=0, column=6, padx=5)\n        self.disconnect_btn = ttk.Button(conn_frame, text=\"Disconnect\", command=self.disconnect, state='disabled')\n        self.disconnect_btn.grid(row=0, column=7, padx=5)\n\n        # Strategy Frame\n        strat_frame = ttk.LabelFrame(root, text=\"Strategy Settings\")\n        strat_frame.pack(fill='x', padx=10, pady=5)\n        ttk.Label(strat_frame, text=\"Symbol:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='w')\n        self.symbol_var = tk.StringVar(value=\"AAPL\")\n        ttk.Entry(strat_frame, textvariable=self.symbol_var, width=8).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(strat_frame, text=\"SecType:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='w')\n        self.sectype_var = sticky='w')\n        self.exchange_var = tk.StringVar(value=\"SMART\")\n        ttk.Entry(strat_frame, textvariable=self.exchange_var, width=8).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        ttk.Label(strat_frame,                         "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import messagebox, ttk\n\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom __init__(self, queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.data_queue = queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.prices = []\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n        self.market_data = {}\n        self.connected_event = threading.Event()\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.connected_event.set()\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        print(f\"Error {reqId} {errorCode} {errorString}\")\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        # Store close prices for momentum calculation\n        if reqId in self.reqId_symbol:\n            symbol = self.reqId_symbol[reqId]\n            if symbol not in self.market_data:\n                self.market_data[symbol] = []\n            self.market_data[symbol].append(bar.close)\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId, start, end):\n        # Notify main thread of new data\n        if reqId in self.reqId_symbol:\n            symbol = self.reqId_symbol[reqId]\n            self.data_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.data_queue.put(('order_status', orderId, status, filled, avgFillPrice))\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.data_queue.put(('exec_details', reqId, execution))\n\n# ========== Momentum Strategy Logic ==========\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    def __init__(self, lookback=10, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold  # 1% move\n\n    def generate_signal(self, prices):\n        if len(prices) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        past_price = prices[-self.lookback-1]\n        current_price = prices[-1]\n        momentum = (current_price - past_price) / past_price\n        if momentum > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif momentum < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# ========== Trading Bot ==========\n\nclass TradingBot(threading.Thread):\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, symbol, exchange, sec_type, currency, queue, interval=60):\n        super().__init__()\n        self.ib = ib\n self.interval = interval\n        self.running = False\n        self.position = 0\n        self.last_signal = 'HOLD'\n        self.order_size = 10  # Default order size, can be set via GUI\n\n    def create_contract(self):\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = self.symbol\n        contract.secType = self.sec_type\n        contract.exchange = self.exchange\n        contract.currency = self.currency\n        return contract\n\n    def request_historical_data(self):\n        reqId = int(time.time() * 1000) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = self.symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[self.symbol] = reqId\n        self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n            reqId,\n            self.create_contract(),\n            \"\",\n            \"2 D\",\n            \"1 min\",\n            \"MIDPOINT\",\n            0, 1, False, []\n        )\n\n    def place_order(self, action):\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = \"MKT\"\n        order.totalQuantity = self.order_size\n        order.transmit = True\n        self.ib.placeOrder(self.ib.nextOrderId, self.create_contract(), order)\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n\n    def run(self):\n        self.running = True\n        while self.running:\n            self.request_historical_data()\n            # Wait for data to be processed\n            try:\n                while True:\n                    msg = self.queue.get(timeout=5)\n                    if msg[0] == 'historical_end' and msg[1] == self.symbol:\n                        break\n            except Empty:\n                print(\"Timeout waiting for historical data.\")\n                continue\n\n            prices = self.ib.market_data.get(self.symbol, [])\n            signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(prices)\n            print(f\"[{self.symbol}] Signal: {signal}\")\n\n            if signal == 'BUY' and self.last_signal != 'BUY':\n                self.place_order('BUY')\n                self.last_signal = 'BUY'\n            elif signal == 'SELL' and self.last_signal != 'SELL':\n                self.place_order('SELL')\n                self.last_signal = 'SELL'\n            else:\n                self.last_signal = 'HOLD'\n\n            # Clear old prices to avoid memory leak\n            self.ib.market_data[self.symbol] = prices[-self.strategy.lookback-1:]\n\n            # Sleep until next interval\n            for _ in range(self.interval):\n                if not self.running:\n                    break\n                time.sleep(1)\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.running = False\n\n# ========== GUI ==========\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    def __init__(self, master):\n        self.master = master\n                     "best_code": "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n        # No need to put in queue here; we'll process after receiving all bars\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # 1% move\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        if not self.ib.nextOrderId:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # Strategy\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Lookback:\").grid(row=2, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.lookback_var = tk.StringVar(value='5')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.lookback_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Threshold (%):\").grid(row=2, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.threshold_var = tk.StringVar(value='1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.threshold_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=3)\n\n        # Start/Stop\n        self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Start Forward Test\", command=self.start_test, state='disabled')\n        self.start_btn.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n        self.stop_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Stop\", command=self.stop_test, state='disabled')\n        self.stop_btn.grid(row=3, column=2, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n\n        # Output\n        self.output = tk.Text(frame, width=90, height=18, state='disabled', bg='#f9f9f9')\n        self.output.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=9, pady=10)\n\n    def connect(self):\n        if self.connected:\n            return\n        host = self.host_var.get()\n        port = int(self.port_var.get())\n        client_id = int(self.client_id_var.get())\n        threading.Thread(target=self._connect, args=(host, port, client_id), daemon=True).start()\n\n    def _connect(self, host, port, client_id):\n        try:\n            self.ib.connect(host, port, client_id)\n            self.ib_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.ib.run, daemon=True)\n            self.ib_thread.start()\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.write_output(f\"Connection error: {e}\")\n\n    def start_test(self):\n        params = dict(\n            symbols=self.symbols_var.get(),\n            bar_size=self.bar_size_var.get(),\n            duration=self.duration_var.get(),\n            quantity=self.qty_var.get(),\n            lookback=self.lookback_var.get(),\n            threshold=str(float(self.threshold_var.get())/100.0)  #                         "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk, messagebox\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    \"\"\"\n    IBApi wraps the IBKR EClient and EWrapper, handles communication and events.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n        # Data is processed after historicalDataEnd\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        # Optional: handle open order events\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # E.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased more than threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased more than threshold\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # 1% move\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    Handles strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    Runs in a separate thread for forward testing.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop:\n        - Requests historical data for each symbol\n        - Waits for data\n        - Generates signals and places orders\n        - Sleeps until next bar\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n#   self.port_var = tk.StringVar(value='7497')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4,        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        \"\"\"Handles errors from IBKR API.\"\"\"\n        self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        \"\"\"Receives historical bar data.\"\"\"\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    Orchestrates the strategy and IBKR API.\n    Handles forward testing: requesting data, generating signals, placing orders.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position \"\"\"Stop forward testing.\"\"\"\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Main bot loop: request data, process signals, place orders.\"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch\nimport threading\nimport queue\n\n# Minimal mock for ibapi BarData-like object\nclass MockBar:\n    def __init__(self, close):\n        self.close = close\n\n# Import classes from the user code\n# For this test, we redefine only the classes we need for testing.\n# Normally, you would import like:\n# from trading_bot import MomentumStrategy, TradingBot, IBApi\n\n# Copy-paste of the relevant classes from the user's code (MomentumStrategy, TradingBot, IBApi)\n# with minor modifications for testability (e.g., removing IBKR dependencies for TradingBot)\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # E.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n\nclass DummyIBApi:\n    \"\"\"A dummy IBApi for TradingBot testing, with minimal stubs.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = 1\n        self.data = {}\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def reqHistoricalData(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        pass\n\n    def placeOrder(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        pass\n\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            # Skipped in test\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            break  # Only run once for testing\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Dummy contract representation for testing\n        return {'symbol': symbol}\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = {'action': action, 'orderType': 'MKT', 'totalQuantity': self.quantity}\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n\nclass TestMomentumStrategy(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy(lookback=3, threshold=0.05)\n\n    def test_hold_on_insufficient_bars(self):\n        bars = [MockBar(100), MockBar(101)]\n        self.assertEqual(self.strategy.generate_signal(bars), 'HOLD')\n\n    def test_buy_signal(self):\n        # Data is processed after historicalDataEnd\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        # Optional: handle open order events\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # E.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        #
