                        "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    \"\"\"\n    IBApi wraps the IBKR EClient and EWrapper, handles communication and events.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}  # symbol: list of bars\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}  # reqId: symbol\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}  # symbol: reqId\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        # IBKR sends errorCode 2104/2106/2108 for info, ignore those\n        if errorCode not in (2104, 2106, 2108):\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            # Bar has .close, .open, .high, .low, .volume, .date\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold  # e.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        if not self.testing:\n            self.testing = True\n            threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            # Request historical data for all symbols\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received (max 10 seconds)\n            wait_time = 0\n            while wait_time < 10:\n                if all(len(self.ib.data.get(sym, [])) > 0 for sym in self.symbols):\n                    break\n                time.sleep(1)\n                wait_time += 1\n\n            # For each symbol, generate signal and possibly place order\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar (bar_size)\n            sleep_sec = self._bar_size_to_seconds(self.bar_size)\n            for _ in range(int(sleep_sec/2)):\n                if not self.testing:\n                    break\n                time.sleep(2)\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol + str(time.time())) % 10000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n    def _bar_size_to_seconds(self, bar_size_str):\n        # Converts bar size string to seconds\n        # e.g. '5 mins' -> 300, '1 min' -> 60\n        bar_size_str = bar_size_str.lower()\n        if 'min' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 60\n        elif 'hour' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 3600\n        elif 'day' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 86400\n        else:\n            return 300  # default 5 min\n\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # Connection row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"TWS Host:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.host_var = tk.StringVar(value='127.0.0.1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.host_var, width=12).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Port:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.port_var = tk.StringVar(value='7497')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4, sticky='e')\n        self.client_id_var = tk.StringVar(value='123')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.client_id_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        self.connect_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Connect\", command=self.connect)\n        self.connect_btn.grid(row=0, column=6, padx=5)\n\n        # Parameters row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Symbols (comma):\").grid(row=1, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.symbols_var = tk.StringVar(value='AAPL,MSFT')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.symbols_var, width=20).grid(row=1, column=1, columnspan=2)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Bar Size:\").grid(row=1, column=3, sticky='e')\n        self.bar_size_var = tk.StringVar(value='5 mins')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.bar_size_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=4)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Duration:\").grid(row=1, column=5, sticky='e')\n        self.duration_var = tk.StringVar(value='2 D')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.duration_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=6)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Qty:\").grid(row=1, column=7, sticky='e')\n        self.qty_var = tk.StringVar(value='10')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.qty_var, width=6).grid(row=1, column=8)\n\n        # Strategy row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Lookback:\").grid(row=2, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.lookback_var = tk.StringVar(value='5')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.lookback_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Threshold (%):\").grid(row=2, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.threshold_var = tk.StringVar(value='1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.threshold_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=3)\n\n        # Start/Stop row\n        self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Start Forward Test\", command=self.start_test, state='disabled')\n        self.start_btn.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n        self.stop_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Stop\", command=self.stop_test, state='disabled')\n        self.stop_btn.grid(row=3, column=2, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n\n        # Output\n        self.output = tk.Text(frame, width=90, height=18, state='disabled', bg='#f9f9f9')\n        self.output.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=9, pady=10)\n\n    def connect(self):\n        if self.connected:\n            return\n        host = self.host_var.get()\n        port = int(self.port_var.get())\n        client_id = int(self.client_id_var.get())\n        threading.Thread(target=self._connect, args=(host, port, client_id), daemon=True).start()\n\n    def _connect(self, host, port, client_id):\n        try:\n            self.ib.connect(host, port, client_id)\n            self.ib_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.ib.run, daemon=True)\n            self.ib_thread.start()\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.write_output(f\"Connection error: {e}\")\n\n    def start_test(self):\n        params = dict(\n            symbols=self.symbols_var.get(),\n            bar_size=self.bar_size_var.get(),\n            duration=self.duration_var.get(),\n            quantity=self.qty_var.get(),\n            lookback=self.lookback_var.get(),\n            threshold=str(float(self.threshold_var.get())/100.0)  # convert % to decimal\n        )\n        self.bot.set_parameters(**params)\n        self.bot.start()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.write_output(\"Started forward testing...\")\n\n    def stop_test(self):\n        self.bot.stop()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.write_output(\"Stopped forward testing.\")\n\n    def write_output(self, msg):\n        self.output['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.output.insert('end', msg + '\\n')\n        self.output.see('end')\n        self.output['state'] = 'disabled'\n\n    def poll_queue(self):\n        try:\n            while True:\n                item = self.app_queue.get_nowait()\n                if item[0] == 'connection':\n                    self.connected = True\n                    self.write_output(\"Connected to IBKR TWS.\")\n                    self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n                elif item[0] == 'error':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Error: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'historical_end':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Historical data received for {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'signal':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Signal: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order_status':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order Status: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'exec_details':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Execution: {item[1]}\")\n        except queue.Empty:\n            pass\n        self.root.after(200, self.poll_queue)\n\n# =========================\n# Main\n# =========================\n\ndef main():\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app = TradingBotGUI(root)\n    root.mainloop()\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()",
                        "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    \"\"\"\n    IBApi wraps the IBKR EClient and EWrapper, handles communication and events.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n        # Data is processed after historicalDataEnd\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        # Optional: handle open order events\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # E.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # Connection\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"TWS Host:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.host_var = tk.StringVar(value='127.0.0.1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.host_var, width=12).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Port:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.port_var = tk.StringVar(value='7497')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4, sticky='e')\n        self.client_id_var = tk.StringVar(value='123')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.client_id_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        self.connect_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Connect\", command=self.connect)\n        self.connect_btn.grid(row=0, column=6, padx=5)\n\n        # Parameters\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Symbols (comma):\").grid(row=1, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.symbols_var = tk.StringVar(value='AAPL,MSFT')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.symbols_var, width=20).grid(row=1, column=1, columnspan=2)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Bar Size:\").grid(row=1, column=3, sticky='e')\n        self.bar_size_var = tk.StringVar(value='5 mins')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.bar_size_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=4)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Duration:\").grid(row=1, column=5, sticky='e')\n        self.duration_var = tk.StringVar(value='2 D')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.duration_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=6)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Qty:\").grid(row=1, column=7, sticky='e')\n        self.qty_var = tk.StringVar(value='10')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.qty_var, width=6).grid(row=1, column=8)\n\n        # Strategy\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Lookback:\").grid(row=2, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.lookback_var = tk.StringVar(value='5')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.lookback_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Threshold (%):\").grid(row=2, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.threshold_var = tk.StringVar(value='1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.threshold_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=3)\n\n        # Start/Stop\n        self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Start Forward Test\", command=self.start_test, state='disabled')\n        self.start_btn.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n        self.stop_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Stop\", command=self.stop_test, state='disabled')\n        self.stop_btn.grid(row=3, column=2, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n\n        # Output\n        self.output = tk.Text(frame, width=90, height=18, state='disabled', bg='#f9f9f9')\n        self.output.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=9, pady=10)\n\n    def connect(self):\n        if self.connected:\n            return\n        host = self.host_var.get()\n        port = int(self.port_var.get())\n        client_id = int(self.client_id_var.get())\n        threading.Thread(target=self._connect, args=(host, port, client_id), daemon=True).start()\n\n    def _connect(self, host, port, client_id):\n        try:\n            self.ib.connect(host, port, client_id)\n            self.ib_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.ib.run, daemon=True)\n            self.ib_thread.start()\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.write_output(f\"Connection error: {e}\")\n\n    def start_test(self):\n        params = dict(\n            symbols=self.symbols_var.get(),\n            bar_size=self.bar_size_var.get(),\n            duration=self.duration_var.get(),\n            quantity=self.qty_var.get(),\n            lookback=self.lookback_var.get(),\n            threshold=str(float(self.threshold_var.get())/100.0)  # convert % to decimal\n        )\n        self.bot.set_parameters(**params)\n        self.bot.start()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.write_output(\"Started forward testing...\")\n\n    def stop_test(self):\n        self.bot.stop()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.write_output(\"Stopped forward testing.\")\n\n    def write_output(self, msg):\n        self.output['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.output.insert('end', msg + '\\n')\n        self.output.see('end')\n        self.output['state'] = 'disabled'\n\n    def poll_queue(self):\n        try:\n            while True:\n                item = self.app_queue.get_nowait()\n                if item[0] == 'connection':\n                    self.connected = True\n                    self.write_output(\"Connected to IBKR TWS.\")\n                    self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n                elif item[0] == 'error':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Error: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'historical_end':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Historical data received for {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'signal':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Signal: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order_status':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order Status: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'exec_details':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Execution: {item[1]}\")\n        except queue.Empty:\n            pass\n        self.root.after(200, self.poll_queue)\n\n# =========================\n# Main\n# =========================\n\ndef main():\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app = TradingBotGUI(root)\n    root.mainloop()\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()",
                        "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    \"\"\"\n    IBApi wraps the IBKR EClient and EWrapper, handles communication and events.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n        # Data is processed after historicalDataEnd\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId, None)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def openOrder(self, orderId, contract, order, orderState):\n        # Optional: handle open order events\n        pass\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold # E.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.positions = {}  # symbol: position size\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        self.testing = True\n        threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received\n            time.sleep(10)  # Give time for IBKR to respond\n\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar\n            time.sleep(60*5)  # 5 minutes\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol) % 1000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # Connection\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"TWS Host:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.host_var = tk.StringVar(value='127.0.0.1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.host_var, width=12).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Port:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.port_var = tk.StringVar(value='7497')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4, sticky='e')\n        self.client_id_var = tk.StringVar(value='123')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.client_id_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        self.connect_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Connect\", command=self.connect)\n        self.connect_btn.grid(row=0, column=6, padx=5)\n\n        # Parameters\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Symbols (comma):\").grid(row=1, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.symbols_var = tk.StringVar(value='AAPL,MSFT')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.symbols_var, width=20).grid(row=1, column=1, columnspan=2)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Bar Size:\").grid(row=1, column=3, sticky='e')\n        self.bar_size_var = tk.StringVar(value='5 mins')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.bar_size_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=4)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Duration:\").grid(row=1, column=5, sticky='e')\n        self.duration_var = tk.StringVar(value='2 D')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.duration_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=6)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Qty:\").grid(row=1, column=7, sticky='e')\n        self.qty_var = tk.StringVar(value='10')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.qty_var, width=6).grid(row=1, column=8)\n\n        # Strategy\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Lookback:\").grid(row=2, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.lookback_var = tk.StringVar(value='5')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.lookback_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Threshold (%):\").grid(row=2, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.threshold_var = tk.StringVar(value='1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.threshold_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=3)\n\n        # Start/Stop\n        self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Start Forward Test\", command=self.start_test, state='disabled')\n        self.start_btn.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n        self.stop_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Stop\", command=self.stop_test, state='disabled')\n        self.stop_btn.grid(row=3, column=2, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n\n        #                         "import unittest\nfrom unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch\nimport threading\nimport queue\n\n# Mock ibapi classes\nclass MockBar:\n    def __init__(self, close, open=0, high=0, low=0, volume=0, date='20230101 12:00:00'):\n        self.close = close\n        self.open = open\n        self.high = high\n        self.low = low\n        self.volume = volume\n        self.date = date\n\nclass MockContract:\n    pass\n\nclass MockOrder:\n    pass\n\n# Import the classes from the user's code\n# We assume the user's code is in a module named trading_bot\n# For demonstration, we'll redefine the classes here as they are above\n\n# Copy-paste the relevant classes from the user's code for testing\n# (MomentumStrategy, TradingBot, IBApi)\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold  # e.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper (minimal mock for TradingBot tests)\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi:\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = 1\n        self.data = {}  # symbol: list of bars\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}\n\n    def reqHistoricalData(self, reqId, contract, endDateTime, durationStr,\n                         barSizeSetting, whatToShow, useRTH, formatDate, keepUpToDate, chartOptions):\n        # Simulate: do nothing, data must be set manually in tests\n        pass\n\n    def placeOrder(self, order_id, contract, order):\n        # Simulate: do nothing\n        pass\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        if not self.testing:\n            self.testing = True\n            threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        # For testing, run only one iteration\n        # Request historical data for all symbols\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n            contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n            self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n            self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                reqId,\n                contract,\n                '',  # now\n                self.duration,\n                self.bar_size,\n                'TRADES',\n                1, 1, False, []\n            )\n        # Wait for all data to be received (simulate immediate for test)\n        # For each symbol, generate signal and possibly place order\n        for symbol in self.symbols:\n            bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n            signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n            self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n            if signal == 'BUY':\n                self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n            elif signal == 'SELL':\n                self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol + str(threading.get_ident())) % 10000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = MockContract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = MockOrder()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n    def _bar_size_to_seconds(self, bar_size_str):\n        # Converts bar size string to seconds\n        # e.g. '5 mins' -> 300, '1 min' -> 60\n        bar_size_str = bar_size_str.lower()\n        if 'min' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 60\n        elif 'hour' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 3600\n        elif 'day' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 86400\n        else:\n            return 300  # default 5 min\n\n# =========================\n# Test Suite\n# =========================\n\nclass TestMomentumStrategy(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy(lookback=3, threshold=0.05)  # 5%\n\n    def test_hold_when_insufficient_bars(self):\n        bars = [MockBar(100), MockBar(101)]\n        self.assertEqual(self.strategy.generate_signal(bars), 'HOLD')\n\n    def test_buy_signal(self):\n        # Price change < threshold\n        bars = [MockBar(100), MockBar(101), MockBar(102), MockBar(104)]\n        self.assertEqual(self.strategy.generate_signal(bars), 'HOLD')\n\n    def test_edge_case_exact_threshold(self):\n        # Exactly at threshold: should not trigger BUY/SELL\n        bars = [MockBar(100), MockBar(101), MockBar(102), MockBar(105)]\n        self.assertEqual(self.strategy.generate_signal(bars), 'HOLD')\n\n    def test_negative_threshold(self):\n        # Negative threshold: should still work\n        self.strategy.threshold = -0.05\n        bars = [MockBar(100), MockBar(102), MockBar(103), MockBar(106)]\n        # Now, ret > threshold (-0.05), so should return BUY\n        self.assertEqual(self.strategy.generate_signal(bars), 'BUY')\n\nclass TestTradingBot(unittest.TestCase):\n    def setUp(self):\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy(lookback=2, threshold=0.10)  #                     "best_code": "import threading\nimport time\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import ttk\nfrom ibapi.client import EClient\nfrom ibapi.wrapper import EWrapper\nfrom ibapi.contract import Contract\nfrom ibapi.order import Order\nimport queue\n\n# =========================\n# IBKR API Client & Wrapper\n# =========================\n\nclass IBApi(EWrapper, EClient):\n    \"\"\"\n    IBApi wraps the IBKR EClient and EWrapper, handles communication and events.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, app_queue):\n        EClient.__init__(self, self)\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.nextOrderId = None\n        self.data = {}  # symbol: list of bars\n        self.reqId_symbol = {}  # reqId: symbol\n        self.symbol_reqId = {}  # symbol: reqId\n\n    def nextValidId(self, orderId: int):\n        self.nextOrderId = orderId\n        self.app_queue.put(('connection', True))\n\n    def error(self, reqId, errorCode, errorString):\n        # IBKR sends errorCode 2104/2106/2108 for info, ignore those\n        if errorCode not in (2104, 2106, 2108):\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', f\"Error {errorCode}: {errorString}\"))\n\n    def historicalData(self, reqId, bar):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId)\n        if symbol:\n            if symbol not in self.data:\n                self.data[symbol] = []\n            # Bar has .close, .open, .high, .low, .volume, .date\n            self.data[symbol].append(bar)\n\n    def historicalDataEnd(self, reqId: int, start: str, end: str):\n        symbol = self.reqId_symbol.get(reqId)\n        if symbol:\n            self.app_queue.put(('historical_end', symbol))\n\n    def orderStatus(self, orderId, status, filled, remaining, avgFillPrice,\n                   permId, parentId, lastFillPrice, clientId, whyHeld, mktCapPrice):\n        self.app_queue.put(('order_status', f\"Order {orderId} status: {status}, filled: {filled}\"))\n\n    def execDetails(self, reqId, contract, execution):\n        self.app_queue.put(('exec_details', f\"Execution: {execution}\"))\n\n\n# =========================\n# Momentum Strategy\n# =========================\n\nclass MomentumStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    Implements a simple momentum strategy:\n    - BUY if price increased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - SELL if price decreased by threshold over lookback bars\n    - HOLD otherwise\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, lookback=5, threshold=0.01):\n        self.lookback = lookback\n        self.threshold = threshold  # e.g. 0.01 for 1%\n\n    def generate_signal(self, bars):\n        # bars: list of BarData (oldest to newest)\n        if len(bars) < self.lookback + 1:\n            return 'HOLD'\n        closes = [bar.close for bar in bars[-(self.lookback+1):]]\n        ret = (closes[-1] - closes[0]) / closes[0]\n        if ret > self.threshold:\n            return 'BUY'\n        elif ret < -self.threshold:\n            return 'SELL'\n        else:\n            return 'HOLD'\n\n\n# =========================\n# Trading Bot Logic\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBot:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBot manages the strategy execution, data requests, and order placement.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, ib, strategy, app_queue):\n        self.ib = ib\n        self.strategy = strategy\n        self.app_queue = app_queue\n        self.testing = False\n        self.symbols = []\n        self.bar_size = '5 mins'\n        self.duration = '2 D'\n        self.quantity = 10\n\n    def set_parameters(self, symbols, bar_size, duration, quantity, lookback, threshold):\n        self.symbols = [s.strip().upper() for s in symbols.split(',') if s.strip()]\n        self.bar_size = bar_size\n        self.duration = duration\n        self.quantity = int(quantity)\n        self.strategy.lookback = int(lookback)\n        self.strategy.threshold = float(threshold)\n\n    def start(self):\n        if not self.testing:\n            self.testing = True\n            threading.Thread(target=self.run, daemon=True).start()\n\n    def stop(self):\n        self.testing = False\n\n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Main trading loop. Requests historical data for each symbol,\n        generates signals, and places orders accordingly.\n        \"\"\"\n        while self.testing:\n            # Request historical data for all symbols\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                reqId = self.get_new_reqId(symbol)\n                contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n                self.ib.data[symbol] = []\n                self.ib.reqHistoricalData(\n                    reqId,\n                    contract,\n                    '',  # now\n                    self.duration,\n                    self.bar_size,\n                    'TRADES',\n                    1, 1, False, []\n                )\n            # Wait for all data to be received (max 10 seconds)\n            wait_time = 0\n            while wait_time < 10:\n                if all(len(self.ib.data.get(sym, [])) > 0 for sym in self.symbols):\n                    break\n                time.sleep(1)\n                wait_time += 1\n\n            # For each symbol, generate signal and possibly place order\n            for symbol in self.symbols:\n                bars = self.ib.data.get(symbol, [])\n                signal = self.strategy.generate_signal(bars)\n                self.app_queue.put(('signal', f\"{symbol}: {signal}\"))\n                if signal == 'BUY':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'BUY')\n                elif signal == 'SELL':\n                    self.place_order(symbol, 'SELL')\n            # Wait for next bar (bar_size)\n            sleep_sec = self._bar_size_to_seconds(self.bar_size)\n            for _ in range(int(sleep_sec/2)):\n                if not self.testing:\n                    break\n                time.sleep(2)\n\n    def get_new_reqId(self, symbol):\n        # Generates a unique request ID for each symbol\n        reqId = hash(symbol + str(time.time())) % 10000000\n        self.ib.reqId_symbol[reqId] = symbol\n        self.ib.symbol_reqId[symbol] = reqId\n        return reqId\n\n    def create_contract(self, symbol):\n        # Creates an IBKR Contract object for a US stock\n        contract = Contract()\n        contract.symbol = symbol\n        contract.secType = 'STK'\n        contract.exchange = 'SMART'\n        contract.currency = 'USD'\n        return contract\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol, action):\n        \"\"\"\n        Places a market order for the specified symbol and action.\n        \"\"\"\n        if self.ib.nextOrderId is None:\n            self.app_queue.put(('error', \"Order ID not ready yet.\"))\n            return\n        contract = self.create_contract(symbol)\n        order = Order()\n        order.action = action\n        order.orderType = 'MKT'\n        order.totalQuantity = self.quantity\n        order.transmit = True\n        order_id = self.ib.nextOrderId\n        self.ib.nextOrderId += 1\n        self.ib.placeOrder(order_id, contract, order)\n        self.app_queue.put(('order', f\"{action} {self.quantity} {symbol} (Order ID: {order_id})\"))\n\n    def _bar_size_to_seconds(self, bar_size_str):\n        # Converts bar size string to seconds\n        # e.g. '5 mins' -> 300, '1 min' -> 60\n        bar_size_str = bar_size_str.lower()\n        if 'min' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 60\n        elif 'hour' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 3600\n        elif 'day' in bar_size_str:\n            return int(bar_size_str.split()[0]) * 86400\n        else:\n            return 300  # default 5 min\n\n\n# =========================\n# GUI Interface\n# =========================\n\nclass TradingBotGUI:\n    \"\"\"\n    TradingBotGUI handles user interaction and displays trading activity.\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, root):\n        self.root = root\n        self.root.title(\"Momentum Trading Bot (IBKR)\")\n        self.app_queue = queue.Queue()\n        self.ib = IBApi(self.app_queue)\n        self.strategy = MomentumStrategy()\n        self.bot = TradingBot(self.ib, self.strategy, self.app_queue)\n        self.connected = False\n\n        self.create_widgets()\n        self.poll_queue()\n\n    def create_widgets(self):\n        frame = ttk.Frame(self.root, padding=10)\n        frame.grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='nsew')\n\n        # Connection row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"TWS Host:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.host_var = tk.StringVar(value='127.0.0.1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.host_var, width=12).grid(row=0, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Port:\").grid(row=0, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.port_var = tk.StringVar(value='7497')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.port_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=3)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Client ID:\").grid(row=0, column=4, sticky='e')\n        self.client_id_var = tk.StringVar(value='123')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.client_id_var, width=6).grid(row=0, column=5)\n        self.connect_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Connect\", command=self.connect)\n        self.connect_btn.grid(row=0, column=6, padx=5)\n\n        # Parameters row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Symbols (comma):\").grid(row=1, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.symbols_var = tk.StringVar(value='AAPL,MSFT')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.symbols_var, width=20).grid(row=1, column=1, columnspan=2)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Bar Size:\").grid(row=1, column=3, sticky='e')\n        self.bar_size_var = tk.StringVar(value='5 mins')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.bar_size_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=4)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Duration:\").grid(row=1, column=5, sticky='e')\n        self.duration_var = tk.StringVar(value='2 D')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.duration_var, width=8).grid(row=1, column=6)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Qty:\").grid(row=1, column=7, sticky='e')\n        self.qty_var = tk.StringVar(value='10')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.qty_var, width=6).grid(row=1, column=8)\n\n        # Strategy row\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Lookback:\").grid(row=2, column=0, sticky='e')\n        self.lookback_var = tk.StringVar(value='5')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.lookback_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=1)\n        ttk.Label(frame, text=\"Threshold (%):\").grid(row=2, column=2, sticky='e')\n        self.threshold_var = tk.StringVar(value='1')\n        ttk.Entry(frame, textvariable=self.threshold_var, width=6).grid(row=2, column=3)\n\n        # Start/Stop row\n        self.start_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Start Forward Test\", command=self.start_test, state='disabled')\n        self.start_btn.grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n        self.stop_btn = ttk.Button(frame, text=\"Stop\", command=self.stop_test, state='disabled')\n        self.stop_btn.grid(row=3, column=2, columnspan=2, pady=8)\n\n        # Output\n        self.output = tk.Text(frame, width=90, height=18, state='disabled', bg='#f9f9f9')\n        self.output.grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=9, pady=10)\n\n    def connect(self):\n        if self.connected:\n            return\n        host = self.host_var.get()\n        port = int(self.port_var.get())\n        client_id = int(self.client_id_var.get())\n        threading.Thread(target=self._connect, args=(host, port, client_id), daemon=True).start()\n\n    def _connect(self, host, port, client_id):\n        try:\n            self.ib.connect(host, port, client_id)\n            self.ib_thread = threading.Thread(target=self.ib.run, daemon=True)\n            self.ib_thread.start()\n        except Exception as e:\n            self.write_output(f\"Connection error: {e}\")\n\n    def start_test(self):\n        params = dict(\n            symbols=self.symbols_var.get(),\n            bar_size=self.bar_size_var.get(),\n            duration=self.duration_var.get(),\n            quantity=self.qty_var.get(),\n            lookback=self.lookback_var.get(),\n            threshold=str(float(self.threshold_var.get())/100.0)  # convert % to decimal\n        )\n        self.bot.set_parameters(**params)\n        self.bot.start()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.write_output(\"Started forward testing...\")\n\n    def stop_test(self):\n        self.bot.stop()\n        self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.stop_btn['state'] = 'disabled'\n        self.write_output(\"Stopped forward testing.\")\n\n    def write_output(self, msg):\n        self.output['state'] = 'normal'\n        self.output.insert('end', msg + '\\n')\n        self.output.see('end')\n        self.output['state'] = 'disabled'\n\n    def poll_queue(self):\n        try:\n            while True:\n                item = self.app_queue.get_nowait()\n                if item[0] == 'connection':\n                    self.connected = True\n                    self.write_output(\"Connected to IBKR TWS.\")\n                    self.start_btn['state'] = 'normal'\n                elif item[0] == 'error':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Error: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'historical_end':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Historical data received for {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'signal':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Signal: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'order_status':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Order Status: {item[1]}\")\n                elif item[0] == 'exec_details':\n                    self.write_output(f\"Execution: {item[1]}\")\n        except queue.Empty:\n            pass\n        self.root.after(200, self.poll_queue)\n\n# =========================\n# Main\n# =========================\n\ndef main():\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app = TradingBotGUI(root)\n    root.mainloop()\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    main()",
